As part of our child safeguarding policy, MovieStarPlanet does not condone the use of the site by adults (those over 18 years). Adults who do not meet the following criteria are not permitted to participate on MovieStarPlanet. An adult is permitted to enter and interact on the site is in the following circumstances:\n•A parent/guardian who is monitoring or helping navigate their child’s use of the site.\n•Law enforcement, journalists, NGO’s or other professions wishing to access the site for educational, law enforcement and research purposes. Access approval (including date and time of participation) is required from the Head of Safety by emailing safety@moviestarplanet.com. \nMovieStarPlanet reserves the right to block any adult from the site it found to be in breach of the above criteria. Refunds will be granted only in the event the user has not violated the game rules.

CARU_PARENT_EMAIL_AFTER_USER_EMAIL_CONFIRMATION=<h2>Your child is now a member at {0}</h2><p>Dear Parent/Legal Guardian<br />Your child has recently registered as member of {0}.<br /><strong>Your child's username is:</strong> {1}<br /><strong>Your child has provided us with the following email address:</strong> {2}</p><p><strong>What is MovieStarPlanet?</strong><br />MovieStarPlanet is a movie themed online game and social network aimed at children aged between 8 and 15 years. On MovieStarPlanet, your child can create Movies, ArtBooks, Looks, clothing designs and other content that can be shared with their movie star friends. Being social is a huge part of tween life and MovieStarPlanet does have chat rooms and forums where players can meet with their friends. However, the online safety of children is and always will be the number one priority for MovieStarPlanet. Children are able to invite their friends to be members of MovieStarPlanet and they may share the friend’s e mail with us. We recommend that that parents follow their child’s online activities and access their child’s account on a regular basis. The will allow parents to share their child’s positive engagement with MovieStarPlanet and monitor who their online friends within the game.</p><p><strong>Parental/Legal Guardian Administration</strong> <br />As the parent or legal guardian, you can control access to the following features:</p><ul> <li>MovieStarPlanet use of your child's e mail address. The e mail will only be used for internal purposes such as if they need to reset their password and news updates about MovieStarPlanet games</li><li>Whether your child can communicate in chat rooms and forums (only users who are level three and above, or VIP members can communicate in the forum)</li><li>Whether your child can view and use the MovieStarPlanet YouTube feature. The YouTube feature has the strictest child filter and is subject to our internal moderation service. We do not share any personal information with YouTube.</li><li>Newsletters with information about the game can be sent to your child if they opt in to this service</li></ul><p>If you would like to disable access to one or all of the above features, please click <a href="{3}" target="_blank">here</a>. Please note that you can only access the link from PC or Mac. If you do not respond to this notice within a limited amount of time, MovieStarPlanet will continue to allow your child access to the above functions.<br /><br />MovieStarPlanet does collect information relating to our player's internet usage. You can request that MovieStarPlanet ceases collection and/or deletes the information relating to your child by contacting our customer support <a href="{7}">here</a>. <br /> <br />If you no longer want your child playing MovieStarPlanet, you can cancel their membership by contacting our customer support <a href="{7}">here</a>. <br /> <br />MovieStarPlanet works hard to ensure the game is a fun and safe environment for children. We have strict automated filtering systems and live moderation for all our online content, including chat rooms and YouTube videos. We do, however, ask that all parents/guardians take an active role in their child’s online presence and read the following sections of our website:</p><ul> <li><a href="{4}" target="_blank">Terms and Conditions</a> </li><li><a href="{5}" target="_blank">Privacy Policy</a> </li><li><a href="{6}" target="_blank">Safety (including how to make a report)</a> </li></ul><p>If you have further questions, please visit our <a href="{7}">Contact</a> page to write to our support staff.</p><p>Please do not reply to this mail.</p><p>Best regards, <br>The MovieStarPlanet Team.</p>

HELP_DESCRIPTION_MORE=<h1>If you need further help</h1><h2>Can’t find an answer?</h2><p>If you can’t find an answer to your question in our Help section, you can either try to ask your fellow movie stars in our forum for help, or contact our support team, who will do their best to get back to you with an answer as soon as possible.</p><h2>Ask in the forum</h2><p>Before you create a topic in the forum and ask for help, be sure to look around and see if your question has already been answered in another topic. Otherwise, our moderators might have to close your topic and your chances of getting a reply will be much smaller.</p><p>When creating your topic, be sure to write a short and precise title, fx “How can I change my password?”, that makes it absolutely clear what you need help with. Then use the post to go into detail with your problem, so your fellow MovieStars can more easily help you and won’t have to ask you questions before they can give an answer.</p><p>In short: the more precise, detailed and short you make your topic, the bigger are the chances that you will get a quick and useful answer.</p><h2>Contact us</h2><p>If you can’t find your answer here or in the forum, you can write to our support team by clicking the “Contact” button in the bottom of the frontpage. Please notice that we can only reply to actual problems, such as technical and billing issues or safety concerns, and that we do not reply to general questions about the game, such as how you earn StarCoins.</p><p>As we receive a lot of support email, it is important that you write us only once and with a precise text, so we can get back to you as quickly as possible. Please mind that during holidays and other specific times, we can receive more emails than usual and therefore will need more time to answer them all. Don’t worry, we will write you back as soon as possible.</p>
HELP_DESCRIPTION_PAYMENT=<h1>Payment Issues</h1><h2>How do I become a VIP?</h2><p>If you are not already a VIP, you buy VIP membership by clicking on the yellow ”become VIP” star in the top right corner. Here you select how long you want to be a VIP and your preferred method of payment. If you are already VIP you can't by more VIP until some days before your present VIP period expires. But you can always buy extra Diamonds and StarCoins.</p><h2>How do I get more Diamonds?</h2><p>Diamonds can only be purchased, either as part of a VIP package or the add-on packages that VIP users get exclusive access to.</p><h2>How do I get more StarCoins?</h2><p>There are two ways: You can earn StarCoins or you can buy StarCoins. To buy StarCoins, click on the “SC” icon on the left side of the top menu, select how many StarCoins you want and pick your payment method.</p><h2>Is it safe to use online payment on MovieStarPlanet?</h2><p>MovieStarPlanet uses a third-party payment provider and for that reason we do not store any credit card or bank account information. All credit card and bank account information is stored, in encrypted form only, by the payment provider at a high security computer centre. All collection and storage of sensitive information by the payment provider conforms to the requirements of the Data Protection Act and complies fully with all international security standards.</p><h2>I can’t buy a VIP membership by sending a SMS with the text “PAY”</h2><p>Instead of replying on the SMS you have received, make a new SMS and send it to the same number with the word “PAY”. Should this fail, please see the section ”My SMS payment failed/didn’t go through”. If this doesn't help please  contact {0}</p><h2>My SMS payment failed/didn’t go through</h2><p>Your SMS payment may have failed due to one or more of the following reasons:</p><ul><li>Your mobile carrier is not supported by BOKU. To check which carriers are supported by BOKU in your country, click on: <a href="http://www.boku.com/support/">http://www.boku.com/support/</a></li><li>You have insufficient funds on your mobile phone.If none of the above applies, please contact us with your username and the name of your mobile carrier, or contact BOKU directly: <a href="http://www.boku.com/help/customer-support//">http://www.boku.com/help/customer-support//</a></li></ul><p></p><h2>What is a spending limit?</h2><p>To ensure that you are not spending too much money, each user profile can only buy StarCoins worth the equivalent of $10/£10 per week using a mobile phone. To prevent you from paying for the profiles of other users, MovieStarPlanet has an additional spending limit on the individual phone number.</p>
HELP_DESCRIPTION_RULES=<h1>Rules & Safety</h1><h2>Rules on MovieStarPlanet (What not to do)</h2><ul><li>\nDo not share your password and do not ask another User for their password. MovieStarPlanet never asks Users for their password, and Users should never reveal their MovieStarPlanet password in any forum, either in-game or outside of the website.</li><li>Do not reveal such details as your real name or password on the promise of a free VIP membership or StarCoins, Diamonds or other prizes/rewards. Nobody needs your password to give you VIP membership or StarCoins, Diamonds or other prizes/rewards.</li><li>Do not reveal personal information (such as real name, email, phone number, age, address, name of school, or user names of Facebook, Skype, MSN etc.) in chatroom, forums, news slider, photos, or other social networking features. However, MovieStarPlanet can add in-game features where your participation requires you to give certain information, on a voluntary basis, e.g. to select your school. You can at any time remove this information.</li><li>Don't write things that are sexually suggestive or racist.</li><li>Don't select a username that refers to gender issues or sexuality, and don't use your real name as your username.</li><li>Don't harass or annoy other users or beg for items. Do not offer other Users items or gift or prizes in exchange for anything.</li><li>Don't use offensive language. Abusive behaviour is not allowed.</li><li>Do not pretend to be or impersonate a staff member/moderator of MovieStarPlanet. A real moderator can be identified by a moderator badge, which will be displayed at all times.</li><li> Do not break or attempt to break any copyright laws.</li><li>Don't send chain letters. Don't copy/paste chain letters.</li><li>Do not talk about how to cheat and do not use cheats to progress in the game. Using cheats, automation software (bots), hacks, or any other unauthorized third-party software designed to modify the Game experience is not allowed</li><li>Don't try to steal or trick items from other users. </li><li> Do not try to steal or trick items from other Users. </li><li> Do not advertise or try to advertise for products or services of commercial interest. </li></ul></p><h2>Do chain letters or cheats work?</h2><p>Chain letters and cheats never work on MovieStarPlanet. Don't trust them, don't copy them and don’t post them! Users who send chain mail run the risk of getting their users deleted. Writing as well as copying chain letters is definitely against the MovieStarPlanet rules!</p><h2>How do I block and unblock users?</h2><p>You can always choose to block users if you don't want them to be able to write you. Just click on a user and then click the Report & Block button (it looks like a “!”). Here you get the option to block a user. In order to remove a blocking, go to Settings in the top-right corner, click "Blocked Users" and then choose the user(s) you want to unblock.</p><h2>How do I report bad behaviour?</h2><p>Report any content you find inappropriate, suspicious or abusive! Please notify us about users who don’t behave on the site. We will then warn or ban this user as quickly as possible. To report a user, click on the user and click the "Report" button (it looks like a “!”). Please explain to us why the user is being reported. Users who are reported for offending other users or abusing MovieStarPlanet may be given a warning, be locked out, or have their accounts deleted.</p><h2>Is it safe to use online payment at MovieStarPlanet?</h2><p>MovieStarPlanet uses a third-party payment provider and for that reason we do not store any credit card or bank account information.  All credit card and bank account information is stored, in encrypted form only, by the payment provider at a high security computer centre. All collection and storage of sensitive information by the payment provider conforms to the requirements of the Data Protection Act and complies fully with all international security standards.</p>
HELP_DESCRIPTION_TECHNICAL=<h1>Technical Help</h1><h2>The site keeps ‘loading’ (Problems with Flash player)</h2><p>If you experience difficulties loading the site, please update your Flash player to the latest version</p><p><a href="http://get.adobe.com/flashplayer/otherversions/">http://get.adobe.com/flashplayer/otherversions/</a></p><h2>Mobile App issues</h2><h3>iPhone, iPod and iPad- users:</h3><p>The iOS-version of MovieStarPlanet is compatible with iPhone 3GS, iPhone 4, iPhone 4S, iPod touch (3rd generation), iPod touch (4th generation) and iPad. It requires iOS 4.0 or later.</p><br><h3>I cannot install the app?</h3><p>Try the following steps:</p><ol><li>Delete the MovieStarPlanet app</li><li>Update your phone to the latest version of iOS</li><li>Install the MovieStarPlanet app again</li></ol><h3>How do I upgrade my version of iOS?</h3><ol><li>Power up the phone and unlock it</li><li>Enter "Settings"</li><li>Enter "General"</li><li>Enter "System Updates"</li><li>Any update for your device will appear here. Click to install it. If no update is showing, and the text "Your software is up to date" is displayed, you cannot update your device further.</li></ol><h3>I updated my phone to the newest version of iOS, and the app still doesn’t work?</h3><p>Your phone might either be A) not supported for installing and using the app, or B) jailbroken, in which case we cannot guarantee that the app works.</p><p>Note: The Android-version of MovieStarPlanet supports only Android-versions 2.2 and higher.</p><p>We do not provide support for specific devices.</p><br><h3>I cannot install the app?</h3><p>Try the following steps:</p><ol><li>Delete the MovieStarPlanet app</li><li>Update your phone to the latest version of Android</li><li>Install the MovieStarPlanet app again</li></ol><h3>How do I upgrade my version of Android?</h3><p>This guide might vary for different version of Android:</p><ol><li>Power up the phone and unlock it</li><li>Enter the menu / list of applications</li><li>Select the "Settings" option Within the "Settings" menu, select the "About phone" option that is found towards the bottom of the list. This option displays the version number and build number of Android that is running on the phone.</li><li>Touch the "System updates" option. This causes the phone to look for any new Android updates. If an update is available, the phone will download and install it.</li></ol><h3>I cannot update Android to a newer version?</h3><p>If the above guide does not work, system updates are not supported by either your mobile carrier or the device manufacturer.  Contact your local Android retailer for more information about this.</p><br><h3>I updated my phone to the newest version of Android, and the app still doesn’t work?</h3><p>Your phone might either be A) not supported for installing and using the app, or B) jailbroken, in which case we cannot guarantee that the app works.</p><br><h3>I don’t have Google Play, I only have Android market - can I still get the app?</h3><p>Google Play is the new name for Android Market, so they’re the same service. Upgrade your phone to the latest version of Android, and you should have Google Play.</p><br><h3>None of the things you said worked – I still cannot use the app?</h3><p>We’re afraid not all phones/devices are supported, due to the underlying technology that enables us to show web-developed MovieStarPlanet content on the phone. Phones lacking compatibility with this technology regrettably cannot run the App.</p>
HELP_DESCRIPTION_USER=<h1>My User</h1><h2>How to keep your password safe</h2><p>Mix letters, numbers and symbols. Pick a password that is at least 6 characters long. Don't use the same password on different sites. Don't give your password information to anyone!</p><h2>What to avoid/what to think about when creating your password</h2><p>Don’t use personal information in your password, such as your birth date and/or name. It should be a long and personal password that no others know about, or can guess because the know you in real life. Never change your password or your email to something that was suggested by others.</p><h2>I can’t log in because someone has taken over my user</h2><p>You only lose an account or items by revealing or trading passwords, by changing to scam email addresses, by entering your password on phishing sites, or by having an easy-to-guess password. MovieStarPlanet urges users to NEVER give out their password to anyone (including those pretending to be MovieStarPlanet staff.) If you still have access to your user, we highly recommend that you change your password immediately: Go to settings, its the cogwheel icon located in the top right corner next to the help icon, and select "Change Password". If someone has changed your password and your email, you can reset your email back to the original by clicking the "Reset password" button below. This will restore your original email on the profile and reset your password. If this doesn’t work, please send us information that proves you are the owner, including any payment references that you might have.</p><h2>I can’t remember my password</h2><p>If you can’t remember your password, click ”Forgot Password” on the front page and enter your email. If you don’t have a confirmed email associated with your user, you will have to write to Support. Remember to send along documentation that this is in fact your user, such as a receipt for purchasing VIP or StarCoins.</p><h2>Change password</h2><p>You change your password in settings. Its the cogwheel icon located in the top right corner next to the help icon. Pick a password that is hard for others to guess, and never share your password with anyone, not even MovieStarPlanet staff. MovieStarPlanet staff will never ask you for your password. If you share your password with others, you risk losing your profile.</p><p><h2>Change username</h2><p>Its unfortunately not possible to change username.</p></p><h2>Associate an email with my user</h2><p>You associate an email with your user in settings. Its the cogwheel icon located in the top right corner next to the help icon. Remember to confirm your email by clicking on the link in the confirmation email you receive from us (and make sure it didn’t end up in your spam folder).</p><h2>Delete my user</h2><p>Login to delete your user. Remember to enter your username correctly – with the right uppercase and lowercase characters.</p>

MSP_PHOTOSHARING_RULES_PERMISSION=The person sharing a photo must first get a permission before sharing a photo of someone else.
MSP_PICTUREUPLOAD_PARENTS=Picture Sharing Safety\r\rThe picture sharing feature within MovieStarPlanet allows users to express themselves and their preferences by sharing images with their friends. We believe this feature is a fun way of incorporating their hobbies, idols and inspirations within the MovieStarPlanet universe. \rIn order to make this feature as safe as possible, we have developed and implemented an extensive list of guidelines to ensure all uploaded content meets our standards. This includes pre-upload moderation of all images submitted for approval, which means that every single image shared by a user will be seen and approved by an adult human moderator before it can be seen on the user's MSP profile. The moderator is able to either approve or reject an image based on clearly defined rules set by the Head of Safety at MovieStarPlanet.\rMoreover, the shared images will be available for viewing by the user and their friends only. \rRules for Picture Sharing\r\rBefore users start using the picture share tool on their mobiles and tablets, the rules of this feature are communicated to them, so that they are made aware of what is acceptable imagery to post on MovieStarPlanet. \rThe user’s image will be deleted if it contains any the following:  \r•	Sexual Content:   Nudity and Partial Nudity (including pictures of users or others in underwear or bathing suits), Sexually Provocative Images, Sexting activity or references to sex\r•	Hate or hate crimes: Racism, Anti-Semitism, religious intolerance, LGBT related hate, sexism and other unacceptable behaviour \r•	Violence: Threats, Actual, Offensive Gestures or Language\r•	Personal Identifiable Information: Names and Address, Tel. Number, e-mail etc., on clothing attire or as collateral information in background of image  \r•	Cyberbullying: Images that portray users in a humiliating or demeaning way  \r•	Cigarettes or reference to smoking: No images that portray children smoking or indicate that smoking is cool  \r•	Alcohol or reference to alcohol: No images with alcohol\r•	Contain drugs, drug paraphernalia, or drug use: No images related to drug use \r•	Any invitations to meet online or offline will not be tolerated: e.g. should we meet, have you got Skype KIK, do you want to have sex, send me some images of yourself \r\rThis list will constantly be checked and updated by our Safety and Support staff, to make sure it encompasses all relevant areas of safety considerations at all times. \rIf a user repeatedly breaks any of the rules set out, they risk being banned, as we do not tolerate inappropriate behavior. They will be notified when their picture has not been approved by the moderators. \rRecommendation for parents\r\rIn all instances, we recommend that parents take an active role when educating children about online safety. When it comes to picture sharing, we suggest parents have an open dialogue about what is acceptable to share online and any potential risks associated with this.

PRIVACY_POLICY_HTML_TEXT_MOBILE_ANALYTICS=<b>Mobile Analytics</b><br>We use mobile analytics software to allow us to better understand the functionality of our Mobile Software on your phone. This software may record information such as how often you use the application, the events that occur within the application, aggregated usage, performance data, and where the application was downloaded from. We do not link the information we store within the analytics software to any personally identifiable information you submit within the mobile application.\n When you download and use our Services, we automatically collect information on the type of device you use, operating system version, and the device identifier (or "UDID").\n<b>Geolocation</b><br>We do not ask for, access or track any location based information from your mobile device at any time while downloading or using our Mobile Apps or Services. \n<b>Push Notifications</b><br>We send you push notifications from time-to-time in order to update you about any events or promotions that we may be running. If you no longer wish to receive these types of communications, you may turn them off at the device level. To ensure you receive proper notifications, we will need to collect certain information about your device such as operating system and user identification information.\n<b>Behavioral Advertising</b><br>We collaborate with a third party either to display advertising on our Web site or to manage advertising on other sites.  Our third party partner may use technologies such as cookies to gather information about your activities on this site and other sites in order to provide you advertising based upon your browsing activities and interests.  If you wish to not have this information used for the purpose of serving you interest-based ads, you may opt-out by clicking here: <a href ="http://preferebces-mgr.truste.com">http://preferebces-mgr.truste.com</a>\nPlease note this does not opt you out of being served ads.  You will continue to receive generic ads.

PRIVACY_POLICY_HTML_TEXT_US_CHILDREN_UNDER_13=<b>Children Under the Age of 13 Years</b><br>MovieStarPlanet is a movie themed online game and social network aimed at children aged between 8 and 15 years. The only personal information we collect from children, under 13, is their email address (to reset the password and send news updates about MovieStarPlanet) and the parents email address to notify their parents that they have joined the site. This email also advises parents that there is the possibility to use chat rooms and forums chat with their friends. We employ trained moderators and "approved lists" that are designed to screen the participation of users under 13 and prevent their disclosure of personally identifiable information in interactive areas of the Website, such as chat rooms.\nIn relation to collecting the information stated above, parents or legal guardians may at any time change the access to or completely opt-out of these socially interactive features. Any such personally identifiable information that is collected, and the required access to change or opt-out, are specified in the direct notice mails sent to the individual Parent or legal guardian. The only personal information we collect from children under 13 is their email address (to reset their password and send news updates about MovieStarPlanet) and their parents email address to notify their parents that they have joined the site.

PRIVACY_POLICY_HTML_TEXT_US_COOKIES=<b>Log files</b><br>As true of most Websites, we gather certain information automatically and store it in log files.  This information may include internet protocol (IP) addresses, browser type, internet service provider (ISP), referring/exit pages, operating system, date/time stamp, and/or clickstream data.  We do not link this automatically collected data to other information we collect about you.\n<b>Tracking Technologies</b><br>Technologies such as: cookies, beacons, tags, and scripts are used by MovieStarPlanet and our partners, affiliates, analytics or service providers. ADTECH technology (see below) is used for this purpose. These analytical tools are used for marketing and internal analytical purposes only to provide better customer support services. We do not collect or store personal information in relation to this data collection   These technologies are used in improving and personalizing your experience at our website, personalize your experience and analyze certain metrics, tell us how many visitors we have on the site, and which parts of the site are most popular, and tracking users' movements around the site and to gather demographic information about our user base as a whole. We may receive reports based on the use of these technologies by these companies on an individual as well as aggregated basis.\nWe use Local Shared Objects, such as Flash cookies, to store content information and preferences. To manage Flash cookies, please click here: <a href=" http://www.macromedia.com/support/documentation/en/flashplayer/help/settings_manager07.html">http://www.macromedia.com/support/documentation/en/flashplayer/help/settings_manager07.html</a>\nThird parties with whom we partner to provide certain features on our website or to display advertising based upon your web browsing activity use HTML5 to collect and store information. Various browsers may offer their own management tools for removing HTML5.\n<b>Advertising</b><br>We are using ADTECH technology, a service provided by ADTECH AG, for ad delivery. We and ADTECH use cookies (text files placed on your computer) to help with collecting information about your visits to this and other websites which may be used in order to provide advertisements about goods and services of interest to you. The information stored in the cookie is used to reference information for standard reporting purposes such as delivered advertising campaigns or banners on websites that are using ADTECH as their ad serving system. Cookie and IP address information of a request to the ADTECH ad serving system is always transferred to the responding data centers in the United States or within the European Union, but only the cookie information of the requested ad domain is stored within the standard records. IP address information is obfuscated after being used to identify attributes associated with the IP address such as location (country, city) or bandwidth. The obfuscating of the IP address leads to anonymization of the data. Upon specific request of a customer, ADTECH provides a special functionality to store IP address information to identify fraudulent activities such as automated click generation systems. You have the option not to participate in ADTECH's analysis by opting out of the use of ADTECH cookies, by selecting the appropriate setting on your browser or setting an ADTECH opt-out cookie provided on the following page <a href ="http://privacy.aol.com/privacy-policy/">http://privacy.aol.com/privacy-policy/</a>. Further information about ADTECH's technology is available under <a href="http://www.adtech.com">http://www.adtech.com</a>. By using this website you consent to the processing of data about you by ADTECH as described herein.

PRIVACY_POLICY_HTML_TEXT_US_DISCLOSING=Users may also choose to disclose personally identifiable information in many interactive areas of the Website if over 13 years of age (See Children Under the Age of 13 years, above). Disclosing personally identifiable information in this way is against the <a href="http://info.moviestarplanet.com/safety/rules.aspx">Rules</a> and users should not do it. The CRISP Automated Content Management System alerts trained Moderators to possible infringements of this rule and sanctions will be applied to users who attempt to circumvent the filters. Once personally identifiable information is made available, it may be collected and used by any person who has access to this content without restriction. If personal information has been disclosed on YouTube, it may be accessible and used by anybody on the Internet. Please note, that once individuals have disclosed such information in this way, it may be impossible to delete it.

All collection and storage of sensitive information by the payment provider conforms to the requirements of the Data Protection Act and fully obliges to all international security standards.  <br/><br/><b>Refunds</b><br/>If you purchase services (including buying Diamonds, StarCoins or virtual goods) you lose any refund rights you may normally be entitled to when the services are made available to you.
